Key Algorithms:\na) Shor\'s Algorithm\n- Purpose: Factor large numbers\n- Classical: O(2ⁿ)\n- Quantum: O(n³)\n- Impact: Could break RSA encryption\n\nb) Grover\'s Algorithm\n- Purpose: Search unstructured data\n- Classical: O(N)\n- Quantum: O(√N)\n- Example: Finding a phone number in an unsorted directory\n\n5. Healthcare Applications:\n- Drug discovery: Simulating molecular interactions\n- Protein folding: Understanding disease mechanisms\n- Treatment optimization: Personalized medicine\n\n6. Current Limitations:\n- Decoherence: Qubits lose information\n- Error rates: Need error correction\n- Scalability: Few stable qubits available\n\nSimple Practice Exercise:\nSimulate a qubit with a pencil:\n1.
